\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
C A\+PI\+: Unicode Properties. 

This C A\+PI provides low-\/level access to the Unicode Character Database. In addition to raw property values, some convenience functions calculate derived properties, for example for Java-\/style programming.

Unicode assigns each code point (not just assigned character) values for many properties. Most of them are simple boolean flags, or constants from a small enumerated list. For some properties, values are strings or other relatively more complex types.

For more information see \char`\"{}\+About the Unicode Character Database\char`\"{} (\href{http://www.unicode.org/ucd/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/ucd/}}) and the I\+CU User Guide chapter on Properties (\href{http://icu-project.org/userguide/properties.html}{\texttt{ http\+://icu-\/project.\+org/userguide/properties.\+html}}).

Many properties are accessible via generic functions that take a U\+Property selector.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2c14623e937b071ff2643d3c3b3f00f4}{u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property()}} returns a binary value (true/false) per property and code point.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a362de15fe826d10e3e45f128ad45f30e}{u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value()}} returns an integer value per property and code point. For each supported enumerated or catalog property, there is an enum type for all of the property\textquotesingle{}s values, and \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a362de15fe826d10e3e45f128ad45f30e}{u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value()}} returns the numeric values of those constants.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ab5434cd00235f76bf323fb39bf8f7566}{u\+\_\+get\+Binary\+Property\+Set()}} returns a set for each I\+C\+U-\/supported binary property with all code points for which the property is true.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a656ada68217db9d29aad2ff24cba7dea}{u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Map()}} returns a map for each I\+C\+U-\/supported enumerated/catalog/int-\/valued property which maps all Unicode code points to their values for that property.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Many functions are designed to match java.\+lang.\+Character functions. See the individual function documentation, and see the J\+DK 1.\+4 java.\+lang.\+Character documentation at \href{http://java.sun.com/j2se/1.4/docs/api/java/lang/Character.html}{\texttt{ http\+://java.\+sun.\+com/j2se/1.\+4/docs/api/java/lang/\+Character.\+html}}

There are also functions that provide easy migration from C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX functions like isblank(). Their use is generally discouraged because the C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX standards do not define their semantics beyond the A\+S\+C\+II range, which means that different implementations exhibit very different behavior. Instead, Unicode properties should be used directly.

There are also only a few, broad C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classes, and they tend to be used for conflicting purposes. For example, the \char`\"{}isalpha()\char`\"{} class is sometimes used to determine word boundaries, while a more sophisticated approach would at least distinguish initial letters from continuation characters (the latter including combining marks). (In I\+CU, Break\+Iterator is the most sophisticated A\+PI for word boundaries.) Another example\+: There is no \char`\"{}istitle()\char`\"{} class for titlecase characters.

I\+CU 3.\+4 and later provides A\+PI access for all twelve C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classes. I\+CU implements them according to the Standard Recommendations in Annex C\+: Compatibility Properties of U\+TS \#18 Unicode Regular Expressions (\href{http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr18/\#Compatibility_Properties}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/reports/tr18/\#\+Compatibility\+\_\+\+Properties}}).

A\+PI access for C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classes is as follows\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item alpha\+: u\+\_\+is\+U\+Alphabetic(c) or u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+A\+L\+P\+H\+A\+B\+E\+T\+I\+C)
\item lower\+: u\+\_\+is\+U\+Lowercase(c) or u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+L\+O\+W\+E\+R\+C\+A\+S\+E)
\item upper\+: u\+\_\+is\+U\+Uppercase(c) or u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+U\+P\+P\+E\+R\+C\+A\+S\+E)
\item punct\+: u\+\_\+ispunct(c)
\item digit\+: u\+\_\+isdigit(c) or u\+\_\+char\+Type(c)==U\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+I\+M\+A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+I\+G\+I\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+ER
\item xdigit\+: u\+\_\+isxdigit(c) or u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+X\+\_\+\+X\+D\+I\+G\+I\+T)
\item alnum\+: u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+X\+\_\+\+A\+L\+N\+U\+M)
\item space\+: u\+\_\+is\+U\+White\+Space(c) or u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+W\+H\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+C\+E)
\item blank\+: u\+\_\+isblank(c) or u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+X\+\_\+\+B\+L\+A\+N\+K)
\item cntrl\+: u\+\_\+char\+Type(c)==U\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+\_\+\+C\+H\+AR
\item graph\+: u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+X\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H)
\item print\+: u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+X\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+N\+T)
\end{DoxyItemize}

Note\+: Some of the u\+\_\+isxyz() functions in \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h}{uchar.\+h}} predate, and do not match, the Standard Recommendations in U\+TS \#18. Instead, they match Java functions according to their A\+PI documentation.



Note\+: There are several I\+CU whitespace functions. Comparison\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item u\+\_\+is\+U\+White\+Space=U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+W\+H\+I\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+CE\+: Unicode White\+\_\+\+Space property; most of general categories \char`\"{}\+Z\char`\"{} (separators) + most whitespace I\+SO controls (including no-\/break spaces, but excluding I\+S1..I\+S4)
\item u\+\_\+is\+Whitespace\+: Java is\+Whitespace; Z + whitespace I\+SO controls but excluding no-\/break spaces
\item u\+\_\+is\+Java\+Space\+Char\+: Java is\+Space\+Char; just Z (including no-\/break spaces)
\item u\+\_\+isspace\+: Z + whitespace I\+SO controls (including no-\/break spaces)
\item u\+\_\+isblank\+: \char`\"{}horizontal spaces\char`\"{} = T\+AB + Zs 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Mask constant for a U\+Char\+Category. @stable I\+CU 2.\+1 \mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a73b5cf593fd2b9113a01fe2680ebd5f6}\label{uchar_8h_a73b5cf593fd2b9113a01fe2680ebd5f6}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{U\_GC\_CN\_MASK}{U\_GC\_CN\_MASK}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define U\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+C\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK~\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a3f694e48867909fbe555586f2b3565be}{U\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a6a2dbc531efce8d77fdb4c314e7fc25ea17181808eb2e207aec907a87472ef550}{U\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+O\+T\+H\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+ES}})}

U\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+X\+X\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK constants are bit flags corresponding to Unicode general category values. For each category, the nth bit is set if the numeric value of the corresponding U\+Char\+Category constant is n.

There are also some U\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK constants for groups of general categories like L for all letter categories.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define U\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})~\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a3f694e48867909fbe555586f2b3565be}{U\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a3333220a7bd943ccb4e9f8ecd0e44a2f}{u\+\_\+char\+Type}}(c))}

Get a single-\/bit bit set for the general category of a character. This bit set can be compared bitwise with U\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+S\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK, U\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK, etc. Same as \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a3f694e48867909fbe555586f2b3565be}{U\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K(u\+\_\+char\+Type(c))}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & the code point to be tested \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a single-\/bit mask corresponding to the general category (U\+Char\+Category) value
\end{DoxyReturn}

The highest Unicode code point value (scalar value) according to The Unicode Standard. This is a 21-\/bit value (20.\+1 bits, rounded up). For a single character, U\+Char32 is a simple type that can hold any code point value.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{src_2skia_2third__party_2externals_2icu_2source_2common_2unicode_2platform_8h_a1fae478cb5a46c7e4a0673d267626696}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+C\+O\+NV}} U\+Char\+Enum\+Type\+Range(const void $\ast$context, \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} start, \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} limit, \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a6a2dbc531efce8d77fdb4c314e7fc25e}{U\+Char\+Category}} type)}

Callback from \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a71ed39034d937e502f82530ddf49d37f}{u\+\_\+enum\+Char\+Types()}}, is called for each contiguous range of code points c (where start$<$=c$<$limit) with the same Unicode general category (\char`\"{}character type\char`\"{}).

The callback function can stop the enumeration by returning false.

\hline
{\em start} & the first code point in a contiguous range with value \\
\hline
{\em limit} & one past the last code point in a contiguous range with value \\
\hline
{\em type} & the general category for all code points in \mbox{[}start..limit\mbox{[} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
false to stop the enumeration
\end{DoxyReturn}

Type of a callback function for \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a8b3265f96b2aeff27f52e3f807ce8379}{u\+\_\+enum\+Char\+Names()}} that gets called for each Unicode character with the code point value and the character name. If such a function returns false, then the enumeration is stopped.

\hline

\hline

\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_aa1da0f88f3370703360231e36a2e3386}\label{uchar_8h_aa1da0f88f3370703360231e36a2e3386}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!UProperty@{UProperty}}
\index{UProperty@{UProperty}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UProperty}{UProperty}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef enum \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}} \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}}}

Selection constants for Unicode properties. These constants are used in functions like u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property to select one of the Unicode properties.

The properties A\+P\+Is are intended to reflect Unicode properties as defined in the Unicode Character Database (U\+CD) and Unicode Technical Reports (U\+TR).

For details about the properties see U\+AX \#44\+: Unicode Character Database (\href{http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr44/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/reports/tr44/}}).

Important\+: If I\+CU is built with U\+CD files from Unicode versions below, e.\+g., 3.\+2, then properties marked with \char`\"{}new in Unicode 3.\+2\char`\"{} are not or not fully available. Check u\+\_\+get\+Unicode\+Version to be sure.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2c14623e937b071ff2643d3c3b3f00f4}{u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a362de15fe826d10e3e45f128ad45f30e}{u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a89603f04ab6abccea48ab30880dd6132}{u\+\_\+get\+Unicode\+Version}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+1

\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!UPropertyNameChoice@{UPropertyNameChoice}}
\index{UPropertyNameChoice@{UPropertyNameChoice}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UPropertyNameChoice}{UPropertyNameChoice}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef enum \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a5056494c7d5a2c7185f3c464f48fe5d1}{U\+Property\+Name\+Choice}} \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a5056494c7d5a2c7185f3c464f48fe5d1}{U\+Property\+Name\+Choice}}}

Selector constants for \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a3209dcbd3669bcc793560b2fa11917d0}{u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Name()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a52dae65fdce1b24d04850c551fa4a5f1}{u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Value\+Name()}}. These selectors are used to choose which name is returned for a given property or value. All properties and values have a long name. Most have a short name, but some do not. Unicode allows for additional names, beyond the long and short name, which would be indicated by U\+\_\+\+L\+O\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME + i, where i=1, 2,...

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2ba37edcca62eff48226e8096035addf}{U\+Char\+Name\+Choice}}}

Selector constants for \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a947055351a58409044369ca956d76281}{u\+\_\+char\+Name()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a947055351a58409044369ca956d76281}{u\+\_\+char\+Name()}} returns the \char`\"{}modern\char`\"{} name of a Unicode character; or the name that was defined in Unicode version 1.\+0, before the Unicode standard merged with I\+S\+O-\/10646; or an \char`\"{}extended\char`\"{} name that gives each Unicode code point a unique name.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}\label{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!UProperty@{UProperty}}
\index{UProperty@{UProperty}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UProperty}{UProperty}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}}}

Selection constants for Unicode properties. These constants are used in functions like u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property to select one of the Unicode properties.

The properties A\+P\+Is are intended to reflect Unicode properties as defined in the Unicode Character Database (U\+CD) and Unicode Technical Reports (U\+TR).

For details about the properties see U\+AX \#44\+: Unicode Character Database (\href{http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr44/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/reports/tr44/}}).

Important\+: If I\+CU is built with U\+CD files from Unicode versions below, e.\+g., 3.\+2, then properties marked with \char`\"{}new in Unicode 3.\+2\char`\"{} are not or not fully available. Check u\+\_\+get\+Unicode\+Version to be sure.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2c14623e937b071ff2643d3c3b3f00f4}{u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a362de15fe826d10e3e45f128ad45f30e}{u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a89603f04ab6abccea48ab30880dd6132}{u\+\_\+get\+Unicode\+Version}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+1 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{UCHAR\_ALPHABETIC@{UCHAR\_ALPHABETIC}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!UCHAR\_ALPHABETIC@{UCHAR\_ALPHABETIC}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199a024fdf3509c03b601694289a4ee5e8ce}\label{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199a024fdf3509c03b601694289a4ee5e8ce}}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{UCHAR\_SEGMENT\_STARTER@{UCHAR\_SEGMENT\_STARTER}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!UCHAR\_SEGMENT\_STARTER@{UCHAR\_SEGMENT\_STARTER}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199a1200d63bfdb0379aa9cdbe8e14d71a26}\label{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199a1200d63bfdb0379aa9cdbe8e14d71a26}} 
U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+G\+M\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+R\+T\+ER&Binary Property Segment\+\_\+\+Starter. I\+C\+U-\/specific property for characters that are starters in terms of Unicode normalization and combining character sequences. They have ccc=0 and do not occur in non-\/initial position of the canonical decomposition of any character (like a-\/umlaut in N\+FD and a Jamo T in an N\+F\+D(\+Hangul L\+V\+T)). I\+CU uses this property for segmenting a string for generating a set of canonically equivalent strings, e.\+g. for canonical closure while processing collation tailoring rules. @stable I\+CU 3.\+0 \\

\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!UPropertyNameChoice@{UPropertyNameChoice}}
\index{UPropertyNameChoice@{UPropertyNameChoice}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UPropertyNameChoice}{UPropertyNameChoice}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a5056494c7d5a2c7185f3c464f48fe5d1}{U\+Property\+Name\+Choice}}}

Selector constants for \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a3209dcbd3669bcc793560b2fa11917d0}{u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Name()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a52dae65fdce1b24d04850c551fa4a5f1}{u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Value\+Name()}}. These selectors are used to choose which name is returned for a given property or value. All properties and values have a long name. Most have a short name, but some do not. Unicode allows for additional names, beyond the long and short name, which would be indicated by U\+\_\+\+L\+O\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME + i, where i=1, 2,...

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a3209dcbd3669bcc793560b2fa11917d0}{u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Name()}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a52dae65fdce1b24d04850c551fa4a5f1}{u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Value\+Name()}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+4 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

U\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+H\+O\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+U\+NT&One more than the highest normal U\+Property\+Name\+Choice value. \begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_charAge()}{u\_charAge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+char\+Age (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uversion_8h_a61caef96ba86d8e86a4031925ea44e94}{U\+Version\+Info}}}]{version\+Array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Get the \char`\"{}age\char`\"{} of the code point. The \char`\"{}age\char`\"{} is the Unicode version when the code point was first designated (as a non-\/character or for Private Use) or assigned a character. This can be useful to avoid emitting code points to receiving processes that do not accept newer characters. The data is from the U\+CD file Derived\+Age.\+txt.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & The code point. \\
\hline
{\em version\+Array} & The Unicode version number array, to be filled in.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
@stable I\+CU 2.\+1 \mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a46ebb7890e8b811f70a86bab359a16e5}\label{uchar_8h_a46ebb7890e8b811f70a86bab359a16e5}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_charDigitValue@{u\_charDigitValue}}
\index{u\_charDigitValue@{u\_charDigitValue}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_charDigitValue()}{u\_charDigitValue()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+char\+Digit\+Value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the decimal digit value of a decimal digit character. Such characters have the general category \char`\"{}\+Nd\char`\"{} (decimal digit numbers) and a Numeric\+\_\+\+Type of Decimal.

Unlike I\+CU releases before 2.\+6, no digit values are returned for any Han characters because Han number characters are often used with a special Chinese-\/style number format (with characters for powers of 10 in between) instead of in decimal-\/positional notation. Unicode 4 explicitly assigns Han number characters the Numeric\+\_\+\+Type Numeric instead of Decimal. See Jitterbug 1483 for more details.

Use u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+E\+R\+I\+C\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E) and \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2923360fe8b92dcc57049fde89b0711f}{u\+\_\+get\+Numeric\+Value()}} for complete numeric Unicode properties.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & the code point for which to get the decimal digit value \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the decimal digit value of c, or -\/1 if c is not a decimal digit character
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2923360fe8b92dcc57049fde89b0711f}{u\+\_\+get\+Numeric\+Value}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a50325108b69e7d08315b5854f85f0593}{U\+Char\+Direction}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+char\+Direction (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the bidirectional category value for the code point, which is used in the Unicode bidirectional algorithm (U\+AX \#9 \href{http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr9/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/reports/tr9/}}). Note that some {\itshape unassigned} code points have bidi values of R or AL because they are in blocks that are reserved for Right-\/\+To-\/\+Left scripts.

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+get\+Directionality()

the bidirectional category (U\+Char\+Direction) value

\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_charFromName@{u\_charFromName}}
\index{u\_charFromName@{u\_charFromName}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_charFromName()}{u\_charFromName()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+char\+From\+Name (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2ba37edcca62eff48226e8096035addf}{U\+Char\+Name\+Choice}}}]{name\+Choice,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{name,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Find a Unicode character by its name and return its code point value. The name is matched exactly and completely. If the name does not correspond to a code point, {\itshape p\+Error\+Code} is set to {\ttfamily U\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+F\+O\+U\+ND}. A Unicode 1.\+0 name is matched only if it differs from the modern name. Unicode names are all uppercase. Extended names are lowercase followed by an uppercase hexadecimal number, and within angle brackets.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em name\+Choice} & Selector for which name to match. \\
\hline
{\em name} & The name to match. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & Pointer to a U\+Error\+Code variable \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The Unicode value of the code point with the given name, or an undefined value if there is no such code point.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2ba37edcca62eff48226e8096035addf}{U\+Char\+Name\+Choice}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_charMirror()}{u\_charMirror()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+char\+Mirror (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Maps the specified character to a \char`\"{}mirror-\/image\char`\"{} character. For characters with the Bidi\+\_\+\+Mirrored property, implementations sometimes need a \char`\"{}poor man\textquotesingle{}s\char`\"{} mapping to another Unicode character (code point) such that the default glyph may serve as the mirror-\/image of the default glyph of the specified character. This is useful for text conversion to and from codepages with visual order, and for displays without glyph selection capabilities.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & the code point to be mapped \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
another Unicode code point that may serve as a mirror-\/image substitute, or c itself if there is no such mapping or c does not have the Bidi\+\_\+\+Mirrored property
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199a72ed372ee7ac1fddb0e7da5d51fae51b}{U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+D\+I\+\_\+\+M\+I\+R\+R\+O\+R\+ED}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a9a85edf1ed9b55cc31be4558ea2a2c18}{u\+\_\+is\+Mirrored}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a947055351a58409044369ca956d76281}\label{uchar_8h_a947055351a58409044369ca956d76281}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_charName@{u\_charName}}
\index{u\_charName@{u\_charName}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_charName()}{u\_charName()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+char\+Name (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{code,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2ba37edcca62eff48226e8096035addf}{U\+Char\+Name\+Choice}}}]{name\+Choice,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{buffer,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{buffer\+Length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Retrieve the name of a Unicode character. Depending on {\ttfamily name\+Choice}, the character name written into the buffer is the \char`\"{}modern\char`\"{} name or the name that was defined in Unicode version 1.\+0. The name contains only \char`\"{}invariant\char`\"{} characters like A-\/Z, 0-\/9, space, and \textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}. Unicode 1.\+0 names are only retrieved if they are different from the modern names and if the data file contains the data for them. gennames may or may not be called with a command line option to include 1.\+0 names in unames.\+dat.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em code} & The character (code point) for which to get the name. It must be {\ttfamily 0$<$=code$<$=0x10ffff}. \\
\hline
{\em name\+Choice} & Selector for which name to get. \\
\hline
{\em buffer} & Destination address for copying the name. The name will always be zero-\/terminated. If there is no name, then the buffer will be set to the empty string. \\
\hline
{\em buffer\+Length} & {\ttfamily ==sizeof(buffer)} \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & Pointer to a U\+Error\+Code variable; check for {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a527f2c69e6b2e3b2c53ad8a99fb36711}{U\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+S\+S()}}} after {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a947055351a58409044369ca956d76281}{u\+\_\+char\+Name()}}} returns. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The length of the name, or 0 if there is no name for this character. If the buffer\+Length is less than or equal to the length, then the buffer contains the truncated name and the returned length indicates the full length of the name. The length does not include the zero-\/termination.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_digit@{u\_digit}}
\index{u\_digit@{u\_digit}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_digit()}{u\_digit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+digit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{ch,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{radix }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the decimal digit value of the code point in the specified radix.

If the radix is not in the range {\ttfamily 2$<$=radix$<$=36} or if the value of {\ttfamily c} is not a valid digit in the specified radix, {\ttfamily -\/1} is returned. A character is a valid digit if at least one of the following is true\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The character has a decimal digit value. Such characters have the general category \char`\"{}\+Nd\char`\"{} (decimal digit numbers) and a Numeric\+\_\+\+Type of Decimal. In this case the value is the character\textquotesingle{}s decimal digit value. 
\item The character is one of the uppercase Latin letters {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}} through {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}Z\textquotesingle{}}. In this case the value is {\ttfamily c-\/\textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}+10}. 
\item The character is one of the lowercase Latin letters {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}} through {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}z\textquotesingle{}}. In this case the value is {\ttfamily ch-\/\textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}+10}. 
\item Latin letters from both the A\+S\+C\+II range (0061..007A, 0041..005A) as well as from the Fullwidth A\+S\+C\+II range (F\+F41..F\+F5A, F\+F21..F\+F3A) are recognized. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+digit().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ch} & the code point to be tested. \\
\hline
{\em radix} & the radix. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the numeric value represented by the character in the specified radix, or -\/1 if there is no value or if the value exceeds the radix.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199a8d7ef62df5dc9907e933f0861d0ba53a}{U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+E\+R\+I\+C\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_afc3ba7ef36c552442e10c519e5280612}{u\+\_\+for\+Digit}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_enumCharNames()}{u\_enumCharNames()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+enum\+Char\+Names (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{start,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{limit,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ace8cef56863951cf15c5552816968c2c}{U\+Enum\+Char\+Names\+Fn}} $\ast$}]{fn,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2ba37edcca62eff48226e8096035addf}{U\+Char\+Name\+Choice}}}]{name\+Choice,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enumerate all assigned Unicode characters between the start and limit code points (start inclusive, limit exclusive) and call a function for each, passing the code point value and the character name. For Unicode 1.\+0 names, only those are enumerated that differ from the modern names.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start} & The first code point in the enumeration range. \\
\hline
{\em limit} & One more than the last code point in the enumeration range (the first one after the range). \\
\hline
{\em fn} & The function that is to be called for each character name. \\
\hline
{\em context} & An arbitrary pointer that is passed to the function. \\
\hline
{\em name\+Choice} & Selector for which kind of names to enumerate. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & Pointer to a U\+Error\+Code variable\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2ba37edcca62eff48226e8096035addf}{U\+Char\+Name\+Choice}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ace8cef56863951cf15c5552816968c2c}{U\+Enum\+Char\+Names\+Fn}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a947055351a58409044369ca956d76281}{u\+\_\+char\+Name}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_af7788cafdd3bd8656e3b3556b1593950}{u\+\_\+char\+From\+Name}} @stable I\+CU 1.\+7 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a71ed39034d937e502f82530ddf49d37f}\label{uchar_8h_a71ed39034d937e502f82530ddf49d37f}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_enumCharTypes@{u\_enumCharTypes}}
\index{u\_enumCharTypes@{u\_enumCharTypes}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_enumCharTypes()}{u\_enumCharTypes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+enum\+Char\+Types (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a992b56937f8bffe6b4f285784da17f57}{U\+Char\+Enum\+Type\+Range}} $\ast$}]{enum\+Range,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{context }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enumerate efficiently all code points with their Unicode general categories.

This is useful for building data structures (e.\+g., Unicode\+Set\textquotesingle{}s), for enumerating all assigned code points (type!=U\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+S\+S\+I\+G\+N\+ED), etc.

For each contiguous range of code points with a given general category (\char`\"{}character type\char`\"{}), the U\+Char\+Enum\+Type\+Range function is called. Adjacent ranges have different types. The Unicode Standard guarantees that the numeric value of the type is 0..31.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enum\+Range} & a pointer to a function that is called for each contiguous range of code points with the same general category \\
\hline

\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_foldCase@{u\_foldCase}}
\index{u\_foldCase@{u\_foldCase}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_foldCase()}{u\_foldCase()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+fold\+Case (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The given character is mapped to its case folding equivalent according to Unicode\+Data.\+txt and Case\+Folding.\+txt; if the character has no case folding equivalent, the character itself is returned.

This function only returns the simple, single-\/code point case mapping. Full case mappings should be used whenever possible because they produce better results by working on whole strings. They take into account the string context and the language and can map to a result string with a different length as appropriate. Full case mappings are applied by the string case mapping functions, see ustring.\+h and the Unicode\+String class. See also the User Guide chapter on C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX migration\+: \href{http://icu-project.org/userguide/posix.html\#case_mappings}{\texttt{ http\+://icu-\/project.\+org/userguide/posix.\+html\#case\+\_\+mappings}}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & the code point to be mapped \\
\hline
{\em options} & Either U\+\_\+\+F\+O\+L\+D\+\_\+\+C\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+A\+U\+LT or U\+\_\+\+F\+O\+L\+D\+\_\+\+C\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+D\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+C\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+I \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the Simple\+\_\+\+Case\+\_\+\+Folding of the code point, if any; otherwise the code point itself. @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_afc3ba7ef36c552442e10c519e5280612}\label{uchar_8h_afc3ba7ef36c552442e10c519e5280612}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_forDigit@{u\_forDigit}}
\index{u\_forDigit@{u\_forDigit}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_forDigit()}{u\_forDigit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+for\+Digit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{digit,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{radix }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines the character representation for a specific digit in the specified radix. If the value of {\ttfamily radix} is not a valid radix, or the value of {\ttfamily digit} is not a valid digit in the specified radix, the null character ({\ttfamily U+0000}) is returned. 

The {\ttfamily radix} argument is valid if it is greater than or equal to 2 and less than or equal to 36. The {\ttfamily digit} argument is valid if {\ttfamily 0 $<$= digit $<$ radix}. 

If the digit is less than 10, then {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{} + digit} is returned. Otherwise, the value {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} + digit -\/ 10} is returned.

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+for\+Digit().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em digit} & the number to convert to a character. \\
\hline
{\em radix} & the radix. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the {\ttfamily char} representation of the specified digit in the specified radix.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Get the F\+C\+\_\+\+N\+F\+K\+C\+\_\+\+Closure property string for a character. See Unicode Standard Annex \#15 for details, search for \char`\"{}\+F\+C\+\_\+\+N\+F\+K\+C\+\_\+\+Closure\char`\"{} or for \char`\"{}\+F\+N\+C\char`\"{}\+: \href{http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr15/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/reports/tr15/}}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & The character (code point) for which to get the F\+C\+\_\+\+N\+F\+K\+C\+\_\+\+Closure string. It must be {\ttfamily 0$<$=c$<$=0x10ffff}. \\
\hline
{\em dest} & Destination address for copying the string. The string will be zero-\/terminated if possible. If there is no F\+C\+\_\+\+N\+F\+K\+C\+\_\+\+Closure string, then the buffer will be set to the empty string. \\
\hline
{\em dest\+Capacity} & {\ttfamily ==sizeof(dest)} \\
\hline
{\em p\+Error\+Code} & Pointer to a U\+Error\+Code variable. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The length of the string, or 0 if there is no F\+C\+\_\+\+N\+F\+K\+C\+\_\+\+Closure string for this character. If the dest\+Capacity is less than or equal to the length, then the buffer contains the truncated name and the returned length indicates the full length of the name. The length does not include the zero-\/termination.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_getIntPropertyMaxValue()}{u\_getIntPropertyMaxValue()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Max\+Value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}}}]{which }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Get the maximum value for an enumerated/integer/binary Unicode property. Can be used together with u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Min\+Value to allocate arrays of Unicode\+Set or similar.

Examples for min/max values (for Unicode 3.\+2)\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+D\+I\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS\+: 0/18 (U\+\_\+\+L\+E\+F\+T\+\_\+\+T\+O\+\_\+\+R\+I\+G\+H\+T/\+U\+\_\+\+B\+O\+U\+N\+D\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+E\+U\+T\+R\+AL)
\item U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+S\+C\+R\+I\+PT\+: 0/45 (U\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+O\+N/\+U\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+\_\+\+T\+A\+G\+B\+A\+N\+WA)
\item U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+D\+E\+O\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+IC\+: 0/1 (false/true)
\end{DoxyItemize}

For undefined U\+Property constant values, min/max values will be 0/-\/1.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em which} & U\+Property selector constant, identifies which binary property to check. Must be U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Maximum value returned by u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value for a Unicode property. $<$=0 if the property selector is out of range.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_getIntPropertyValue@{u\_getIntPropertyValue}}
\index{u\_getIntPropertyValue@{u\_getIntPropertyValue}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_getIntPropertyValue()}{u\_getIntPropertyValue()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}}}]{which }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Get the property value for an enumerated or integer Unicode property for a code point. Also returns binary and mask property values.

Unicode, especially in version 3.\+2, defines many more properties than the original set in Unicode\+Data.\+txt.

The properties A\+P\+Is are intended to reflect Unicode properties as defined in the Unicode Character Database (U\+CD) and Unicode Technical Reports (U\+TR). For details about the properties see \href{http://www.unicode.org/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/}} . For names of Unicode properties see the U\+CD file Property\+Aliases.\+txt.

Sample usage\+: U\+East\+Asian\+Width ea=(U\+East\+Asian\+Width)u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+E\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+A\+S\+I\+A\+N\+\_\+\+W\+I\+D\+T\+H); U\+Bool b=(U\+Bool)u\+\_\+get\+Int\+Property\+Value(c, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+D\+E\+O\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+I\+C);


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & Code point to test. \\
\hline
{\em which} & U\+Property selector constant, identifies which property to check. Must be U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Numeric value that is directly the property value or, for enumerated properties, corresponds to the numeric value of the enumerated constant of the respective property value enumeration type (cast to enum type if necessary). Returns 0 or 1 (for false/true) for binary Unicode properties. Returns a bit-\/mask for mask properties. Returns 0 if \textquotesingle{}which\textquotesingle{} is out of bounds or if the Unicode version does not have data for the property at all, or not for this code point.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a15493bbbc3793fa60b33cad4955430a0}{U\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+I\+S\+O\+Comment (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{dest,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{dest\+Capacity,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{utypes_8h_a3343c1c8a8377277046774691c98d78c}{U\+Error\+Code}} $\ast$}]{p\+Error\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns an empty string. Used to return the I\+SO 10646 comment for a character. The Unicode I\+S\+O\+\_\+\+Comment property is deprecated and has no values.

{\em dest} & Destination address for copying the comment. The comment will be zero-\/terminated if possible. If there is no comment, then the buffer will be set to the empty string. \\

{\em dest\+Capacity} & {\ttfamily ==sizeof(dest)} \\

\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_getNumericValue@{u\_getNumericValue}}
\index{u\_getNumericValue@{u\_getNumericValue}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_getNumericValue()}{u\_getNumericValue()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} double U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+Numeric\+Value (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Get the numeric value for a Unicode code point as defined in the Unicode Character Database.

A \char`\"{}double\char`\"{} return type is necessary because some numeric values are fractions, negative, or too large for int32\+\_\+t.

For characters without any numeric values in the Unicode Character Database, this function will return U\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+E\+R\+I\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+L\+UE. Note\+: This is different from the Unicode Standard which specifies NaN as the default value. (NaN is not available on all platforms.)

Similar to java.\+lang.\+Character.\+get\+Numeric\+Value(), but \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a2923360fe8b92dcc57049fde89b0711f}{u\+\_\+get\+Numeric\+Value()}} also supports negative values, large values, and fractions, while Java\textquotesingle{}s get\+Numeric\+Value() returns values 10..35 for A\+S\+C\+II letters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & Code point to get the numeric value for. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Numeric value of c, or U\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+E\+R\+I\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+L\+UE if none is defined.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a0358d9cce8fdd3255867affe2a8b21ff}{U\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+E\+R\+I\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+L\+UE}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+2 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a9f662d5df732fe74ba8fa85543d0230d}\label{uchar_8h_a9f662d5df732fe74ba8fa85543d0230d}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_getPropertyEnum@{u\_getPropertyEnum}}
\index{u\_getPropertyEnum@{u\_getPropertyEnum}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_getPropertyEnum()}{u\_getPropertyEnum()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Enum (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{alias }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Return the U\+Property enum for a given property name, as specified in the Unicode database file Property\+Aliases.\+txt. Short, long, and any other variants are recognized.

In addition, this function maps the synthetic names \char`\"{}gcm\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+General\+\_\+\+Category\+\_\+\+Mask\char`\"{} to the property U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK. These names are not in Property\+Aliases.\+txt.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em alias} & the property name to be matched. The name is compared using \char`\"{}loose matching\char`\"{} as described in Property\+Aliases.\+txt.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a U\+Property enum, or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+DE if the given name does not match any property.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+4 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_getPropertyName()}{u\_getPropertyName()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} char$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Name (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}}}]{property,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a5056494c7d5a2c7185f3c464f48fe5d1}{U\+Property\+Name\+Choice}}}]{name\+Choice }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Return the Unicode name for a given property, as given in the Unicode database file Property\+Aliases.\+txt.

In addition, this function maps the property U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK to the synthetic names \char`\"{}gcm\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+General\+\_\+\+Category\+\_\+\+Mask\char`\"{}. These names are not in Property\+Aliases.\+txt.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em property} & U\+Property selector other than U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+DE. If out of range, N\+U\+LL is returned.\\
\hline
{\em name\+Choice} & selector for which name to get. If out of range, N\+U\+LL is returned. All properties have a long name. Most have a short name, but some do not. Unicode allows for additional names; if present these will be returned by U\+\_\+\+L\+O\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME + i, where i=1, 2,...\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a pointer to the name, or N\+U\+LL if either the property or the name\+Choice is out of range. If a given name\+Choice returns N\+U\+LL, then all larger values of name\+Choice will return N\+U\+LL, with one exception\+: if N\+U\+LL is returned for U\+\_\+\+S\+H\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME, then U\+\_\+\+L\+O\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME (and higher) may still return a non-\/\+N\+U\+LL value. The returned pointer is valid until \mbox{\hyperlink{uclean_8h_a02cee2494284801dcc7f8bf7f12f0bcd}{u\+\_\+cleanup()}} is called.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a5056494c7d5a2c7185f3c464f48fe5d1}{U\+Property\+Name\+Choice}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+4

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_getPropertyValueEnum()}{u\_getPropertyValueEnum()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} int32\+\_\+t U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Value\+Enum (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}}}]{property,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{alias }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Return the property value integer for a given value name, as specified in the Unicode database file Property\+Value\+Aliases.\+txt. Short, long, and any other variants are recognized.

Note\+: Some of the names in Property\+Value\+Aliases.\+txt will only be recognized with U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK, not U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY. These include\+: \char`\"{}\+C\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Other\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+L\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Letter\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+L\+C\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Cased\+\_\+\+Letter\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+M\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Mark\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+N\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Number\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+P\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Punctuation\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+S\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Symbol\char`\"{}, and \char`\"{}\+Z\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Separator\char`\"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em property} & U\+Property selector constant. Must be U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT. If out of range, U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+DE is returned.\\
\hline
{\em alias} & the value name to be matched. The name is compared using \char`\"{}loose matching\char`\"{} as described in Property\+Value\+Aliases.\+txt.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a value integer or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+DE if the given name does not match any value of the given property, or if the property is invalid. Note\+: U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK values are not values of U\+Char\+Category, but rather mask values produced by \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a6def30b7d6d22c7de63c2a80596ee847}{U\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K()}}. This allows grouped categories such as \mbox{[}\+:L\+:\mbox{]} to be represented.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} char$\ast$ U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+Property\+Value\+Name (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}}}]{property,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a5056494c7d5a2c7185f3c464f48fe5d1}{U\+Property\+Name\+Choice}}}]{name\+Choice }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Return the Unicode name for a given property value, as given in the Unicode database file Property\+Value\+Aliases.\+txt.

Note\+: Some of the names in Property\+Value\+Aliases.\+txt can only be retrieved using U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK, not U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY. These include\+: \char`\"{}\+C\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Other\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+L\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Letter\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+L\+C\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Cased\+\_\+\+Letter\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+M\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Mark\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+N\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Number\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+P\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Punctuation\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+S\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Symbol\char`\"{}, and \char`\"{}\+Z\char`\"{} / \char`\"{}\+Separator\char`\"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em property} & U\+Property selector constant. Must be U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT or U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT. If out of range, N\+U\+LL is returned.\\
\hline
{\em value} & selector for a value for the given property. If out of range, N\+U\+LL is returned. In general, valid values range from 0 up to some maximum. There are a few exceptions\+: (1.) U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+L\+O\+CK values begin at the non-\/zero value U\+B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+L\+A\+T\+IN. (2.) U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+C\+A\+N\+O\+N\+I\+C\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+B\+I\+N\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+SS values are not contiguous and range from 0..240. (3.) U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK values are not values of U\+Char\+Category, but rather mask values produced by \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a6def30b7d6d22c7de63c2a80596ee847}{U\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+K()}}. This allows grouped categories such as \mbox{[}\+:L\+:\mbox{]} to be represented. Mask values range non-\/contiguously from 1..U\+\_\+\+G\+C\+\_\+\+P\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK.\\
\hline
{\em name\+Choice} & selector for which name to get. If out of range, N\+U\+LL is returned. All values have a long name. Most have a short name, but some do not. Unicode allows for additional names; if present these will be returned by U\+\_\+\+L\+O\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME + i, where i=1, 2,...\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a pointer to the name, or N\+U\+LL if either the property or the name\+Choice is out of range. If a given name\+Choice returns N\+U\+LL, then all larger values of name\+Choice will return N\+U\+LL, with one exception\+: if N\+U\+LL is returned for U\+\_\+\+S\+H\+O\+R\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME, then U\+\_\+\+L\+O\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+P\+E\+R\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+N\+A\+ME (and higher) may still return a non-\/\+N\+U\+LL value. The returned pointer is valid until \mbox{\hyperlink{uclean_8h_a02cee2494284801dcc7f8bf7f12f0bcd}{u\+\_\+cleanup()}} is called.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_getUnicodeVersion@{u\_getUnicodeVersion}}
\index{u\_getUnicodeVersion@{u\_getUnicodeVersion}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_getUnicodeVersion()}{u\_getUnicodeVersion()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} void U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+get\+Unicode\+Version (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uversion_8h_a61caef96ba86d8e86a4031925ea44e94}{U\+Version\+Info}}}]{version\+Array }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets the Unicode version information. The version array is filled in with the version information for the Unicode standard that is currently used by I\+CU. For example, Unicode version 3.\+1.\+1 is represented as an array with the values \{ 3, 1, 1, 0 \}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em version\+Array} & an output array that will be filled in with the Unicode version number @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a2c14623e937b071ff2643d3c3b3f00f4}\label{uchar_8h_a2c14623e937b071ff2643d3c3b3f00f4}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_hasBinaryProperty@{u\_hasBinaryProperty}}
\index{u\_hasBinaryProperty@{u\_hasBinaryProperty}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_hasBinaryProperty()}{u\_hasBinaryProperty()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+has\+Binary\+Property (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_ae40d616419e74ecc7c80a9febab03199}{U\+Property}}}]{which }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Check a binary Unicode property for a code point.

Unicode, especially in version 3.\+2, defines many more properties than the original set in Unicode\+Data.\+txt.

The properties A\+P\+Is are intended to reflect Unicode properties as defined in the Unicode Character Database (U\+CD) and Unicode Technical Reports (U\+TR). For details about the properties see \href{http://www.unicode.org/ucd/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/ucd/}} . For names of Unicode properties see the U\+CD file Property\+Aliases.\+txt.

Important\+: If I\+CU is built with U\+CD files from Unicode versions below 3.\+2, then properties marked with \char`\"{}new in Unicode 3.\+2\char`\"{} are not or not fully available.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & Code point to test. \\
\hline
{\em which} & U\+Property selector constant, identifies which binary property to check. Must be U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+RT$<$=which$<$U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+N\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+L\+I\+M\+IT. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true or false according to the binary Unicode property value for c. Also false if \textquotesingle{}which\textquotesingle{} is out of bounds or if the Unicode version does not have data for the property at all, or not for this code point.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+isalnum (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines whether the specified code point is an alphanumeric character (letter or digit) according to Java. True for characters with general categories \char`\"{}\+L\char`\"{} (letters) and \char`\"{}\+Nd\char`\"{} (decimal digit numbers).

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+is\+Letter\+Or\+Digit().

In addition to being equivalent to a Java function, this also serves as a C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX migration function. See the comments about C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classification functions in the documentation at the top of this header file.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+isbase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Non-\/standard\+: Determines whether the specified code point is a base character. True for general categories \char`\"{}\+L\char`\"{} (letters), \char`\"{}\+N\char`\"{} (numbers), \char`\"{}\+Mc\char`\"{} (spacing combining marks), and \char`\"{}\+Me\char`\"{} (enclosing marks).

Note that this is different from the Unicode Standard definition in chapter 3.\+6, conformance clause D51 \+Base character, which defines base characters as the code points with general categories Letter (L), Number (N), Punctuation (P), Symbol (S), or Space Separator (Zs).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_isblank()}{u\_isblank()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+isblank (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines whether the specified code point is a \char`\"{}blank\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}horizontal space\char`\"{}, a character that visibly separates words on a line. The following are equivalent definitions\+:

true for Unicode White\+\_\+\+Space characters except for \char`\"{}vertical space controls\char`\"{} where \char`\"{}vertical space controls\char`\"{} are the following characters\+: U+000A (LF) U+000B (VT) U+000C (FF) U+000D (CR) U+0085 (N\+EL) U+2028 (LS) U+2029 (PS)

same as

true for U+0009 (T\+AB) and characters with general category \char`\"{}\+Zs\char`\"{} (space separators).

Note\+: There are several I\+CU whitespace functions; please see the \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h}{uchar.\+h}} file documentation for a detailed comparison.

This is a C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX migration function. See the comments about C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classification functions in the documentation at the top of this header file.

{\em c} & the code point to be tested \\

\end{DoxyParams}

true if the code point is a \char`\"{}blank\char`\"{}
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+iscntrl (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines whether the specified code point is a control character (as defined by this function). A control character is one of the following\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item I\+SO 8-\/bit control character (U+0000..U+001f and U+007f..U+009f)
\item U\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+\_\+\+C\+H\+AR (Cc)
\item U\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+AR (Cf)
\item U\+\_\+\+L\+I\+N\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+OR (Zl)
\item U\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+G\+R\+A\+P\+H\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+OR (Zp)
\end{DoxyItemize}

This is a C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX migration function. See the comments about C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classification functions in the documentation at the top of this header file.

true if the code point is a control character

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+isdefined (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines whether the specified code point is \char`\"{}defined\char`\"{}, which usually means that it is assigned a character. True for general categories other than \char`\"{}\+Cn\char`\"{} (other, not assigned), i.\+e., true for all code points mentioned in Unicode\+Data.\+txt.

Note that non-\/character code points (e.\+g., U+\+F\+D\+D0) are not \char`\"{}defined\char`\"{} (they are Cn), but surrogate code points are \char`\"{}defined\char`\"{} (Cs).

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+is\+Defined().

Determines if the specified character should be regarded as an ignorable character in an identifier, according to Java. True for characters with general category \char`\"{}\+Cf\char`\"{} (format controls) as well as non-\/whitespace I\+SO controls (U+0000..U+0008, U+000E..U+001B, U+007F..U+009F).

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+is\+Identifier\+Ignorable().

Note that Unicode just recommends to ignore Cf (format controls).

Determines if the specified character is permissible in an identifier according to Java. True for characters with general categories \char`\"{}\+L\char`\"{} (letters), \char`\"{}\+Nl\char`\"{} (letter numbers), \char`\"{}\+Nd\char`\"{} (decimal digits), \char`\"{}\+Mc\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}\+Mn\char`\"{} (combining marks), \char`\"{}\+Pc\char`\"{} (connecting punctuation), and u\+\_\+is\+I\+D\+Ignorable(c).

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+is\+Unicode\+Identifier\+Part(). Almost the same as Unicode\textquotesingle{}s I\+D\+\_\+\+Continue (U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+I\+D\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+I\+N\+UE) except that Unicode recommends to ignore Cf which is less than u\+\_\+is\+I\+D\+Ignorable(c).

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+is\+Java\+Space\+Char (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determine if the specified code point is a space character according to Java. True for characters with general categories \char`\"{}\+Z\char`\"{} (separators), which does not include control codes (e.\+g., T\+AB or Line Feed).

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+is\+Space\+Char().

Note\+: There are several I\+CU whitespace functions; please see the \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h}{uchar.\+h}} file documentation for a detailed comparison.

\index{u\_islower@{u\_islower}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_islower()}{u\_islower()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+islower (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines whether the specified code point has the general category \char`\"{}\+Ll\char`\"{} (lowercase letter).

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+is\+Lower\+Case().

This misses some characters that are also lowercase but have a different general category value. In order to include those, use U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+L\+O\+W\+E\+R\+C\+A\+SE.

In addition to being equivalent to a Java function, this also serves as a C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX migration function. See the comments about C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classification functions in the documentation at the top of this header file.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & the code point to be tested \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the code point is an Ll lowercase letter
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+isupper (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines whether the specified code point has the general category \char`\"{}\+Lu\char`\"{} (uppercase letter).

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+is\+Upper\+Case().

This misses some characters that are also uppercase but have a different general category value. In order to include those, use U\+C\+H\+A\+R\+\_\+\+U\+P\+P\+E\+R\+C\+A\+SE.

In addition to being equivalent to a Java function, this also serves as a C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX migration function. See the comments about C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classification functions in the documentation at the top of this header file.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & the code point to be tested \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the code point is an Lu uppercase letter
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_isUWhiteSpace()}{u\_isUWhiteSpace()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+is\+U\+White\+Space (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a04f065643431b3709133a19241ab2901}\label{uchar_8h_a04f065643431b3709133a19241ab2901}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_isWhitespace@{u\_isWhitespace}}
\index{u\_isWhitespace@{u\_isWhitespace}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_isWhitespace()}{u\_isWhitespace()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+is\+Whitespace (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines if the specified code point is a whitespace character according to Java/\+I\+CU. A character is considered to be a Java whitespace character if and only if it satisfies one of the following criteria\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It is a Unicode Separator character (categories \char`\"{}\+Z\char`\"{} = \char`\"{}\+Zs\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}\+Zl\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}\+Zp\char`\"{}), but is not also a non-\/breaking space (U+00\+A0 N\+B\+SP or U+2007 Figure Space or U+202F Narrow N\+B\+SP).
\item It is U+0009 H\+O\+R\+I\+Z\+O\+N\+T\+AL T\+A\+B\+U\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON.
\item It is U+000A L\+I\+NE F\+E\+ED.
\item It is U+000B V\+E\+R\+T\+I\+C\+AL T\+A\+B\+U\+L\+A\+T\+I\+ON.
\item It is U+000C F\+O\+RM F\+E\+ED.
\item It is U+000D C\+A\+R\+R\+I\+A\+GE R\+E\+T\+U\+RN.
\item It is U+001C F\+I\+LE S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+OR.
\item It is U+001D G\+R\+O\+UP S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+OR.
\item It is U+001E R\+E\+C\+O\+RD S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+OR.
\item It is U+001F U\+N\+IT S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+OR.
\end{DoxyItemize}

This A\+PI tries to sync with the semantics of Java\textquotesingle{}s java.\+lang.\+Character.\+is\+Whitespace(), but it may not return the exact same results because of the Unicode version difference.

Note\+: Unicode 4.\+0.\+1 changed U+200B Z\+E\+RO W\+I\+D\+TH S\+P\+A\+CE from a Space Separator (Zs) to a Format \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_control}{Control}} (Cf). Since then, is\+Whitespace(0x200b) returns false. See \href{http://www.unicode.org/versions/Unicode4.0.1/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+unicode.\+org/versions/\+Unicode4.\+0.\+1/}}

Note\+: There are several I\+CU whitespace functions; please see the \mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h}{uchar.\+h}} file documentation for a detailed comparison.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & the code point to be tested \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the code point is a whitespace character according to Java/\+I\+CU
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a968ff9ad1f2b56f726ed981c35c4c1dd}{u\+\_\+isspace}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a4a2dc82717cbd94e923ca005121cac3a}{u\+\_\+is\+Java\+Space\+Char}} 

\mbox{\hyperlink{uchar_8h_a7f6861b56df683880043fa1574384212}{u\+\_\+is\+U\+White\+Space}} @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a377f6b60008d8a6d3818e21cc4124e29}\label{uchar_8h_a377f6b60008d8a6d3818e21cc4124e29}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_isxdigit@{u\_isxdigit}}
\index{u\_isxdigit@{u\_isxdigit}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_isxdigit()}{u\_isxdigit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a349ef00011f20ccd1d3b424445681aa5}{U\+Bool}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+isxdigit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Determines whether the specified code point is a hexadecimal digit. This is equivalent to u\+\_\+digit(c, 16)$>$=0. True for characters with general category \char`\"{}\+Nd\char`\"{} (decimal digit numbers) as well as Latin letters a-\/f and A-\/F in both A\+S\+C\+II and Fullwidth A\+S\+C\+II. (That is, for letters with code points 0041..0046, 0061..0066, F\+F21..F\+F26, F\+F41..F\+F46.)

In order to narrow the definition of hexadecimal digits to only A\+S\+C\+II characters, use (c$<$=0x7f \&\& u\+\_\+isxdigit(c)).

This is a C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX migration function. See the comments about C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX character classification functions in the documentation at the top of this header file.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & the code point to be tested \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the code point is a hexadecimal digit
\end{DoxyReturn}
@stable I\+CU 2.\+6 \mbox{\Hypertarget{uchar_8h_a4fd8dac00e886ae027fc05ade376f9d1}\label{uchar_8h_a4fd8dac00e886ae027fc05ade376f9d1}} 
\index{uchar.h@{uchar.h}!u\_tolower@{u\_tolower}}
\index{u\_tolower@{u\_tolower}!uchar.h@{uchar.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{u\_tolower()}{u\_tolower()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a676114b1a64bb7c2de15c919a00b28df}{U\+\_\+\+C\+A\+PI}} \mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}} U\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+O\+R\+T2 u\+\_\+tolower (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{umachine_8h_a09fff5c3b5a5b015324dc3ec3cf92809}{U\+Char32}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The given character is mapped to its lowercase equivalent according to Unicode\+Data.\+txt; if the character has no lowercase equivalent, the character itself is returned.

Same as java.\+lang.\+Character.\+to\+Lower\+Case().

This function only returns the simple, single-\/code point case mapping. Full case mappings should be used whenever possible because they produce better results by working on whole strings. They take into account the string context and the language and can map to a result string with a different length as appropriate. Full case mappings are applied by the string case mapping functions, see ustring.\+h and the Unicode\+String class. See also the User Guide chapter on C/\+P\+O\+S\+IX migration\+: \href{http://icu-project.org/userguide/posix.html\#case_mappings}{\texttt{ http\+://icu-\/project.\+org/userguide/posix.\+html\#case\+\_\+mappings}}

{\em c} & the code point to be mapped \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the Simple\+\_\+\+Lowercase\+\_\+\+Mapping of the code point, if any; otherwise the code point itself. @stable I\+CU 2.\+0 
\end{DoxyReturn}
